```python
import requests
import csv

# Your Supabase REST API URL
url = "https://hfvirholjjkiswqsvadm.supabase.co/rest/v1/profiles?select=*"

# Headers using your tokens
headers = {
    "apikey": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6ImhmdmlyaG9sampraXN3cXN2YWRtIiwicm9sZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3NzU1NzA5MzEsImV4cCI6MjA5MTE0NjkzMX0.cNdzMixH1hTqJS5J6_E7jZr7OGJTdCWM2WG-WCj3wNc",
    "authorization": "Bearer eyJhbGciOiJFUzI1NiIsImtpZCI6ImExMmJlNWZlLTdiNTItNGUyOC1iNzgzLTM0OWY5Y2JkOWU4OSIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJodHRwczovL2hmdmlyaG9sampraXN3cXN2YWRtLnN1cGFiYXNlLmNvL2F1dGgvdjEiLCJzdWIiOiI3YWMzZjgzMS1mOWU1LTQ4YWQtYjYxZi00NTY0Y2U5ZjEyMjQiLCJhdWQiOiJhdXRoZW50aWNhdGVkIiwiZXhwIjoxNzgwNTYyMjk1LCJpYXQiOjE3ODA1NTg2OTUsImVtYWlsIjoiYm9saXk1MTUxN0A1bmVrLmNvbSIsInBob25lIjoiIiwiYXBwX21ldGFkYXRhIjp7InByb3ZpZGVyIjoiZW1haWwiLCJwcm92aWRlcnMiOlsiZW1haWwiXX0sInVzZXJfbWV0YWRhdGEiOnsiYXZhdGFyX3VybCI6ImF2YXRhcjEiLCJlbWFpbCI6ImJvbGl5NTE1MTdANW5lay5jb20iLCJlbWFpbF92ZXJpZmllZCI6dHJ1ZSwicGhvbmVfdmVyaWZpZWQiOmZhbHNlLCJzdWIiOiI3YWMzZjgzMS1mOWU1LTQ4YWQtYjYxZi00NTY0Y2U5ZjEyMjQiLCJ1c2VybmFtZSI6ImNpc2NvIn0sInJvbGUiOiJhdXRoZW50aWNhdGVkIiwiYWFsIjoiYWFsMSIsImFtciI6W3sibWV0aG9kIjoicGFzc3dvcmQiLCJ0aW1lc3RhbXAiOjE3ODA1NTg2OTV9XSwic2Vzc2lvbl9pZCI6IjYxNTBhNjBmLWJhZmYtNDhjOC05YzMzLTY0NWUxNzU4MjgwMiIsImlzX2Fub255bW91cyI6ZmFsc2V9.d4rzMMcKVq7oJxJSWq9cVRqBTxrsy_YyDj8-UuqTR4tiVRAdBQcA150KBXZbmsWliJ9Mh9V-wPivP8y7DCSAuA",
    "accept": "application/json"
}

all_profiles = []
limit = 1000  # Fetch 1000 records at a time
offset = 0

print("Fetching data from Supabase...")

# 1. LOOP TO FETCH ALL PAGES
while True:
    # Add limit and offset as URL parameters
    params = {
        "limit": limit,
        "offset": offset
    }
    
    response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params)
    
    if response.status_code == 200:
        batch = response.json()
        
        # If the batch is empty, we have reached the end of the database
        if not batch:
            break
            
        all_profiles.extend(batch)
        print(f"Fetched {len(batch)} records... (Total downloaded: {len(all_profiles)})")
        
        # Increase the offset for the next loop
        offset += limit
    else:
        print(f"Failed to fetch data. Status code: {response.status_code}")
        print(f"Error message: {response.text}")
        break

# 2. EXPORT TO CSV
if all_profiles:
    csv_filename = "supabase_profiles.csv"
    
    # Get the column names (headers) from the keys of the very first dictionary
    csv_columns = list(all_profiles[0].keys())
    
    # Open the file and write the data
    with open(csv_filename, mode='w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as csv_file:
        writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=csv_columns)
        
        writer.writeheader() # Write column names
        for profile in all_profiles:
            writer.writerow(profile) # Write each user's data
            
    print(f"\n✅ Success! Exported {len(all_profiles)} profiles to '{csv_filename}'.")
else:
    print("\nNo data was found to export.")
```
